The main goal is to improve student's expeience in eSports disciplines. The club will provide training in teams, developing all important skills to become a better player. Potentially our goal is to participate in tournametns as a university representative.

We already have Overwatch, Dota 2 and CS GO disciplines. And we are open for new games. If you are good at Hearthstone, Quake, OSU or any other competetive game and you want to become a coach at that discipline please pm to @fairwale.
